## p. 5 (#9) ################################################

Foreword
This is the first edition of the Directory of Providers of Services-
Hospitals. A similar directory is available for home health agencies
participating in the Health Insurance for the Aged Program. The
directory for extended care facilities will be available after April l967.
This directory is a compilation of the names and addresses of hospitals,
which are participating as providers of services in the Health Insurance
for the Aged Program. It was prepared to furnish identifying information
regarding the availability of hospital services covered under Title XVIII
of the Social Security Act.
For this purpose, a provider of service is a hospital which (l) meets
certain requirements under the Health Insurance for the Aged Act and (2)
has entered into an agreement with the Secretary of the Department of
Health, Education, and Welfare to provide services to Health Insurance
beneficiaries.
To facilitate reference the directory is arranged in alphabetical
sequence by State; by city within State; and by the name of the hospital.
This compilation of providers of services is based on Social Security
Administration records as of January l, l967. It is planned to reissue
this directory every sjy Tn"ri't'Vlg . or as required, depending on the number
of hospitals which have changed designations or which have become
providers of services since the date of the previous publication.
Bureau of Health Insurance
Social Security Administration
Department of Health, Education, and Welfare
